98:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":["Two adapters, not one, ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"contributorAdapter"}]," for lint-class rules, ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"formatContributorAdapter"}]," for format-class. 99:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Why two parallel interfaces?"}]," The engine’s internal ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"Rule"}]," is allowed to evolve freely; the public ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"rule.Rule"}]," is the stability boundary contributors compile against.
